<script>
//<![CDATA[
function manipulationOfCart(product, type, list) {
	if (list == undefined){
		list='Category - '+ product.category
	}
	console.log(list);
	ga('ec:addProduct', {
        'id': product.id,
        'name': product.name,
        'category': product.category,
        'brand': product.brand,
        'variant': product.variant,
        'price': product.price,
		'list': list,
        'quantity': product.qty
    });
	
    ga('ec:setAction', type, {list: list});
	
	
    if (type == 'add')
    {
		        ga('send', 'event', 'UX', 'click', 'Add To Cart - ' + product.name, {'nonInteraction': 1});
    }
    else if (type == 'remove')
    {
		        ga('send', 'event', 'UX', 'click', 'Remove From Cart - ' + product.name, {'nonInteraction': 1});
    }
}

jQuery(document).ready(function($){
    $.cookie.json = true;
	    var productToBasket = $.cookie("productToBasket");
	var productlist = $.cookie("productlist");

    if (productToBasket != undefined)
    {
        //console.log(productToBasket);
        manipulationOfCart(productToBasket, 'add', productlist);
        $.removeCookie("productToBasket", { path: '/', domain: '.www.konga.com'});
		$.removeCookie("productlist", { path: '/', domain: '.www.konga.com'});
    }

    var productOutBasket = $.cookie("productOutBasket");

    if (productOutBasket != undefined)
    {
        manipulationOfCart(productOutBasket, 'remove', '');
        $.removeCookie("productOutBasket", { path: '/', domain: '.www.konga.com' });
    }
});
//]]>
</script>

        function facebookPopup() {
            FB.getLoginStatus(function(response) {
                if (response.status == 'connected') {
                    facebookLogin();
                } else {
                    FB.login(function(response) {
                        if (response.authResponse) {
                            facebookLogin();
                        }
                    }, {scope: 'email'});
                }
            });
        }

        }
    }

<script>
    jQuery(document).ready(function(e){
        jQuery('#searchsuggestion_list').unbind('click').bind('click', function( event ) {
            var text = jQuery.trim(jQuery(event.target).closest('.searchsuggestion_item').text());
            var inPosition = text.indexOf(' in ');
            if (inPosition > 0) {
                text = text.substr(0, inPosition);
            }
            jQuery('#search').val(text);
        });
    });
</script>

        jQuery('#search_mini_form').removeAttr("autocomplete");
        jQuery('.search-submit').click(function(){
            if( jQuery('#search').val() == 'Search entire store here...'){
                jQuery('#search').addClass('error')
                    .delay(10000)
                    .queue(function(){
                        jQuery(this).removeClass("error");
                        jQuery(this).dequeue();
                    });
                jQuery('#search').click(function(){
                    jQuery('#search').removeClass("error");
                    jQuery('#search').dequeue();
                })
            } else {
                jQuery('#search_mini_form').submit();
            }
        })
        jQuery( "#search" ).bind('keypress', function(e) {
            var code = e.keyCode || e.which;
            if(code == 13) { //Enter keycode
                jQuery('#search_mini_form').submit();
                e.preventDefault();
            }
        });
        </script>
    </div>
</form>

<script>
    //Arrange menu
    var menu = jQuery('#menu'),
        columnCount = 3;

    //Order by column
    if(menu.children().length) {
        for(var i = 1; i <= columnCount; i++) {
            var subCat = menu.find('.col-' + i);

            targetCat = subCat.parents('.inner').find('> ul:nth-child(' + i + ')');
            subCat.appendTo(targetCat);
        }
    }

    //Order by position
    // 1st level
    //menu.children('li').tsort({data: 'order'});
    // 2nd level
    menu.find('.inner > ul > li').tsort({data: 'order'});
    // 3rd level
    menu.find('.inner > ul > li > ul > li').tsort({data: 'order'});

    jQuery(document).ready(function(){

        if(!jQuery(".konga-menu-cover").length)
        {
            jQuery("<div class='konga-menu-cover'></div>").prependTo("body");
        }

        var kongaMenyCover = jQuery(".konga-menu-cover");

        jQuery("#konga-menu #menu").hover(
            function() {
                jQuery(kongaMenyCover).addClass("is-hover");
            }, function() {
                jQuery(kongaMenyCover).removeClass("is-hover");
            }
        );
    });
</script>            </div>

    //Arrange menu
    var menu = jQuery('#menu'),
        columnCount = 3;

    //Order by column
    if(menu.children().length) {
        for(var i = 1; i <= columnCount; i++) {
            var subCat = menu.find('.col-' + i);

            targetCat = subCat.parents('.inner').find('> ul:nth-child(' + i + ')');
            subCat.appendTo(targetCat);
        }
    }

    //Order by position
    // 1st level
    //menu.children('li').tsort({data: 'order'});
    // 2nd level
    menu.find('.inner > ul > li').tsort({data: 'order'});
    // 3rd level
    menu.find('.inner > ul > li > ul > li').tsort({data: 'order'});
